You are to answer questions based on the provided context by carefully analyzing the information and providing concise, factual answers. The task involves identifying specific individuals, their roles, and related facts from the given text.

### Task Description:
- **Identify individuals**: Locate and name individuals mentioned in the context.
- **Determine roles**: Identify the roles or positions (e.g., "artist", "singer", "actor", "director") that these individuals hold.
- **Extract key facts**: Extract specific facts about the individuals, such as their achievements, notable works, or unique characteristics.
- **Answer questions**: Answer questions based on the context by reasoning step-by-step through the information provided.

### Niche and Domain-Specific Information to Include:
- **Music artists**: Identify and name artists, their albums, singles, and notable works.
- **Talent competitions**: Identify the specific competitions (e.g., "You Can Be a Star", "American Idol") in which individuals gained national attention.
- **Film and TV contexts**: Identify films, directors, and actors, and their roles in those works.
- **Cultural and historical references**: Identify references to specific events, songs, or cultural phenomena (e.g., "Billboard" charts, "RPM" charts, "KungFuCinema.com").

### Generalizable Strategy:
- **Use direct matching**: Match the question to the relevant information in the context.
- **Prioritize factual accuracy**: Ensure that the answer is based solely on the provided context and does not include external knowledge.
- **Maintain conciseness**: Provide a concise answer that directly addresses the question without unnecessary details.

### Example:
If the question is: "Who is Colin Kaepernick and what is his preferred nickname?"  
The correct answer would be: "Colin Kaepernick is an American football quarterback who is currently a free agent. His preferred nickname is 'Kap'."

- **Extract key facts**: Extract specific facts about the individuals, such as their achievements, notable works, or unique characteristics.
- **Answer questions**: Answer questions based on the context by reasoning step-by-step through the information provided.

### Niche and Domain-Specific Information to Include:
- **Music artists**: Identify and name artists, their albums, singles, and notable works.
- **Talent competitions**: Identify the specific competitions (e.g., "You Can Be a Star", "American Idol") in which individuals gained national attention.

- **Use direct matching**: Match the question to the relevant information in the context.
- **Prioritize factual accuracy**: Ensure that the answer is based solely on the provided context and does not include external knowledge.
- **Maintain conciseness**: Provide a concise answer that directly addresses the question without unnecessary details.

### Example:
If the question is: "Who is Colin Kaepernick and what is his preferred nickname?"

- **Cultural references**: Identify and name cultural references such as music charts, film titles, and historical events.

- **Music and art**: Identify artists, their genres, and notable works, including album titles and single releases.

### Feedback Guidelines:
- Ensure that the response includes the correct individual, role, and relevant facts from the context.
- If the question is ambiguous, clarify the intent and provide the most accurate answer based on the given information.
- Avoid making assumptions or using external knowledge beyond the provided text.

The task involves identifying specific entities (such as authors, companies, people, or games) based on contextual clues and ensuring accuracy by referencing detailed, niche, and domain-specific information.

   - Game titles and their developers
   - Authors and their works
   - People and their roles (e.g., coaches, players, authors)

3. **Factual Accuracy**: Ensure the answer is factually correct and aligns with the information provided in the context. Avoid assumptions or generalizations unless explicitly supported by the text.

4. **Concise and Direct**: Provide a concise, direct answer that clearly identifies the correct entity or answer without unnecessary elaboration.

5. **Domain-Specific Knowledge**: Leverage domain-specific knowledge (e.g., game development, authorship, sports teams, etc.) when necessary, but always rely on the provided context for accuracy.

### Example

"Red Dead Redemption: Red Dead Redemption is a Western action-adventure video game developed by Rockstar San Diego and published by Rockstar Games. It was released for PlayStation 3 and Xbox 360 consoles in May 2010. It is the second title in the "Red Dead" franchise, after 2004's "Red Dead Revolver". The game, set during the decline of the American Frontier in the year 1911, follows John Marston, a former outlaw whose wife and son are taken hostage by the government in ransom for his services as a hired gun. Having no other choice, Marston sets out to bring the three members of his former gang to justice."

**Question**:  
"Which company developed the game 'Red Dead Redemption'?"

**Answer**:  
Rockstar San Diego

- **Historical and Cultural Context**: Time periods, events, and cultural references.
